 1256 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      2 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | * Create_Sprite — Compiled sprite engine
 1257 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      3 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | * Ported from FTA's CREATE.SPRITE.S (1989)
 1258 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      4 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | *
 1259 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      5 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | * Compiles shape data into native 65816 code that
 1260 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      6 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | * draws sprites via direct-page writes to SHR shadow RAM.
 1261 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      7 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | *
 1262 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      8 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | * Call: copy sprite table ($18 bytes) to bank $00 direct page,
 1263 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      9 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | *       LDA #dp_address / JSR Create_Sprite
 1264 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     10 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | *
 1265 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     11 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | * Sprite table format (24 bytes at DP offsets $00-$17):
 1266 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     12 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | *   $00 ADRL Rout_Adr    — output: where compiled code is written
 1267 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     13 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/08A3               | *   $04 ADRL Shape_Adr   — input: shape pixel data (24-bit)
